## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="45ca1-918">Attributs Windows Server 2008 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="45ca1-918">Windows Server 2008 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="45ca1-919">Cette classe contient les attributs suivants pour Windows Server 2008 R2 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="45ca1-919">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="45ca1-1787">Notes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="45ca1-1787">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="45ca1-1788">La classe **MS-DFSR-subscription** fait partie de la prise en charge du service de réplication système de fichiers DFS (DFS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="45ca1-1788">The **ms-DFSR-Subscription** class is a part of the Distributed File System (DFS) Replication service support.</span></span>
